<rating>5< /rating><text>Flower City is one of those little treasures you love having in your neighborhood. They don't deliver, but they do fast and usually accurate take away. You can eat in, though they're very small. However, the food is always worth it, wherever you decide to consume it. My favorite appetizers are the brandy chicken wings and the potstickers, though a close third would be their crab Rangoon. They are one of the few places where I equally like the noodle dishes and the rice dishes, and their wonton soup is my husband's favorite. Still, pretty much everything I've had there thus far has been great, although on a few occasions the egg rolls have come out a little greasier than I like, but one of my best friends always seems to love them, so that may just be my particular palate. Whatever you have, I highly recommend Flower City restaurant for really great Chinese food and always friendly service from their staff.< /text><Pictures>None</Pictures>< Response>

< text>
Great place to buy affordable Taiwanese pastries and cakes. Sheng Kee Bakery has been in Skyline Plaza for 20 years, which is incredible. Customer service is OK. My favorite pastries to buy here are the Pineapple Bun, Custard Bun, Pork Sung Bun, Egg Tart, and Chocolate Twist. Their cakes absolutely creamy and the presentation is perfect for birthdays or other special occasions.

Personally, I haven't tried the coffee here, which is a partnership with Peet's, but my mom has and she doesn't care for it.< /text>

< review>
Pickup was great; fast and easy, nice guys. Scheduling was a bit of a miscommunication. While originally told it would be a 2-hour window, which is standard, when I finally set up my date (based on new furniture delivery date), I asked if they could be there early am, like by 8:30. I was told that would be fine, we would be the first stop.
Day of, not so much. I called to relay which parking lot to use at my dad's apartment complex, and was told I had a 10-12 arrival window. This was a problem, because the new furniture was coming within a window that started at 8:45. It was taking away old couch before delivery of new. For my dad's senior apartment, where that's the only seating. Didn't want to leave him for 24 hours or more with no place to sit but his bed, and no room for a second couch!
But Junk Kings was able to divert a crew my way, they arrived before the new couch, and everything worked out. I would use them again, hopefully for a less complex situation...< /review>
